After completing his official duties, he will have to return to his hometown of Littrow Chau and then return to the Philippines to resume his duties.

Shanghai Citizens' National Products Association 119

Yesterday, hosted the press.

Issued a declaration and a letter to the citizens.

The Shanghai Citizens' National Products Association hosted reporters from various newspapers at the Industrial and Commercial Research Society on the second floor of Taichangfang, Zhejiang Road, at 3:00 PM yesterday. More than twenty people attended, and members of the association, including Wu Jiangdong, Hu Shaomei, and Zhu Jiandong, provided courteous hospitality on the scene. The details are recorded as follows:

Chairman's Report 120

First, Chairman Zheng Jianbo reported the purpose of the meeting and the significance of organizing this association, stating briefly that the purpose of the associates forming this association is to promote national products by setting an example, and to promote the consistent use of national products by all citizens of the city. Don’t just pay lip service, but do it in practice, to fulfill the national duty of the people. He stated that he had participated in the work of the Volunteer Army in the past, organized the Northeast Four Provinces Transportation Corps, all of which were patriotic movements. This time, forming an association to promote national products is also based on the concept of patriotism. Hard work is the key. In short, patriotic movements within the legal framework will not be obstructed by anyone and can proceed smoothly. He hoped that the press would provide assistance, etc. Then, Hu Shaomei and others gave speeches successively, and distributed national product cigarettes and refreshments produced by the China Merchants People's Tobacco Company before the meeting ended.

Declaration Issued 121

The association issued a declaration yesterday, saying: Since the Opium War, China has traded with Western countries. Due to the restrictions of unequal treaties, tariffs are not independent, so that foreign goods can be imported with only a small amount of tariffs, and can be unimpeded. In recent years, the import of foreign goods has become more and more rampant, with an annual trade deficit of more than 300 million yuan. Natural disasters and man-made disasters at home have been frequent, and the rural economy has been bankrupted, and it is almost impossible to recover. In addition, the loss of the three northeastern provinces and Rehe has sharply reduced agricultural exports, and the purchasing power of the people is becoming increasingly low. Since 1920, the world economic depression has gradually spread around the globe, and industrial countries have launched economic struggles, devaluing currency prices, building tariff barriers, and dumping goods. As a result, Chinese markets are flooded with foreign goods, and domestic factories are in a world economic panic, and the collapse of the domestic rural economy, under the dual oppression, is already dying. It has also been attacked by the annexation policies of various countries, like fallen leaves swept away by the autumn wind. Therefore, the closure of industrial and commercial enterprises is almost daily, and the national economy is becoming more and more empty due to the large outflow of cash over the years. If this continues, the country will not be a country. However, if the skin is gone, what will the hair be attached to? The call for promoting national products by the people of the country, from the May 30th Movement to the present, has been working hard to implement it, and it has been popular for a while, but so far no results have been seen. It is only because the people's hearts are depraved, and they have been intoxicated with foreign goods for a long time, and they compete for luxury, and they are ashamed to use national products. Although the call for promoting national products has reached the clouds, due to the accumulated burden, it is still of no help. The associates, based on the late Premier’s teachings, in view of the creation of the New Life Movement, the failure of past promoters of national products, and for the sake of stabilizing the national economy and the prosperity of rural life, under the principle of self-sufficiency, developing domestic industry and commerce, in order to save the situation and stop the leakage. It is hoped that in the world economic depression, the country will survive. The associates have a patriotic heart, and they have no way to save the poor. They are willing to set an example, use national products, set the tone first, and advocate the trend. Therefore, the Shanghai Citizens National Products Association is organized to persuade all walks of life in the city to use national products. The associates do not feel ashamed of their own insignificance, and they are encouraged to encourage themselves, adhering to the courage to move forward, the spirit of perseverance, and strive to implement, to fulfill their national duties. I hope that all institutions, all groups, and people from all walks of life will guide them and work together to complete the work. Then the national industry will be fortunate, and the future of national products will really rely on it. We hereby declare.

Letter to the Citizens 122

The association respectfully informs the citizens, saying: Dear comrades and compatriots, in this world economic gloom that cages the Chinese national economy, it is exactly like being exposed to wind and rain, and the arrival of the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident has shattered the Chinese people's attempt to gradually pass the prosperous illusion. In this critical moment of survival, we should use all our strength to reverse our own destiny. Living in a drunken life and dreaming of death is not how we can live our lives. The paper image of singing and dancing has been torn apart by the power of the times. Now the Dongcha incident is another powerful bomb. The collapse of the national rural economy, the various problems of banditry and foreign insults, all have the possibility of turning us from a semi-colonial place into a non-two-price colony. And judging from the trade reports of the customs over the years, since the eleventh year of the Republic of China, it has been necessary to average more than 300 to 400 million yuan every year. This big leak tightens us and falls into a position of eternal doom. Compatriots, please don’t be infatuated anymore and rely on the strength of others to consolidate yourself. There is absolutely no such beautiful ideal in the world that can become a reality. We must understand that "only our own strength can save ourselves." This is an unchanging rule for thousands of years. The associates feel the current crisis in China, and individual abilities are weak. Therefore, we want to start with our own practical and effective self-help methods, that is, to use national products in our daily life, restore rights, and strive to develop national industry and commerce and survive under the self-sufficient nationalist economy. Compatriots, I hope that with the power of the public, we can support the growth of our small contribution, and in Shanghai, which holds the economic lifeline of the whole country, we can reap great results. Compatriots who are determined to save the country, please be able to implement it faithfully, swear faithfully, and everyone rises up together to protect the beloved motherland of the Republic of China!

China Aviation Association 123

Actively preparing for the second solicitation.

According to the Central News Agency, since the fourth plenary meeting of the board of directors of the China Aviation Association resolved to invite Mayor Wu to serve as the commander-in-chief, the association will hold a second solicitation of members in the city, and continue to collect membership fees and raise funds for the aviation rescue fund. It is reported that Li Dachao, the chief executive of the commander-in-chief's office, is following the instructions of the commander-in-chief, and has begun to plan the direction of the campaign, and is supervising the various cadres to rush to handle various solicitation procedures day and night. Office Rules 124

The rules of the Shanghai Solicitation Team Commander-in-Chief's Office of the China Aviation Association, Article 1, The China Aviation Association, in order to extensively solicit members, continue to collect membership fees, and raise funds for aviation rescue, has established the Shanghai Solicitation Team Commander-in-Chief's Office. Article 2, The purpose of the solicitation of this office is to promote air defense construction, support the expansion of the air force, and develop civil aviation. Article 3, This office is set up with two staff officers and one chief executive, who handle solicitation and fundraising matters under the command of the commander-in-chief. Article 4, This office is divided into five groups: general affairs, finance, solicitation, fundraising, and propaganda. Each group is set up with several cadres and employees, who handle matters of their respective groups under the command of the chief executive. Article 5, This office will hold an office meeting once a week, and temporary meetings may be convened when necessary. Article 6, The implementation plan and detailed rules of this office will be formulated separately. Article 7, These rules will be implemented on the date of approval by the commander-in-chief.

Implementation Plan 125

Outline of the implementation plan of the Shanghai Solicitation Team Commander-in-Chief's Office of the China Aviation Association, 1. This office has formulated the outline of the implementation plan in order to organize solicitation, fundraising, and propaganda, and to facilitate implementation and achieve practical results. 2. The goals of this office's solicitation are to reach 100,000 new members and an aviation rescue fund of 1 million yuan. 3. Organize 500 solicitation teams in the city. The captains are appointed by the commander-in-chief, and each team has a number of members, who are selected and appointed by the captain. 4. Each solicitation team will solicit at least 1,000 members, or more than 5,000 yuan in membership fees, or more than 5,000 yuan in donations. 5. The solicitation period is from January 28th, 24th year to the end of July, for a period of six months. 6. The scope of solicitation includes those who have already been solicited to join the association, and continue to collect membership fees. Regardless of the personnel of families, shops, companies, banks, money houses, factories, schools, or other institutions, and their relatives, friends, men, women, old and young, workers, etc., should be solicited to join the association. 7. Fundraising must be done in such a way that everyone actively donates and fully supports aviation to save the country. 8. Fundraising should have detailed and effective methods, and be promoted in various ways. 9. Propaganda should be universal, popular, and stimulating, and be able to generate power, so that the public can understand and pay attention to it. 10. Propaganda should enable influential people to jointly awaken people from all walks of life to recognize that aviation to save the country is the only way today, so that the public can actively participate. 11. Propaganda methods should focus on effectiveness, with the most economical way to achieve the greatest effectiveness. The target is the majority of the people, such as leaflets, slogans, drawings, speeches, news, etc. 13. This outline will be implemented after approval by the commander-in-chief.

Awards 126

The award methods of the Shanghai Solicitation Team of China Aviation Association, 1. Trophy: Whoever solicits the most members or donates the most donations, in addition to being awarded medals and listed on the monument, will be specially made by the association and presented with a trophy. 2. Medal: All captains and team members who solicit and raise enough or exceed the quota, such as the captain soliciting more than 1,000 members, collecting more than 5,000 yuan in membership fees, or raising more than 5,000 yuan, and team members soliciting more than 100 members, collecting more than 500 yuan in membership fees, or raising more than 1,000 yuan, in addition to being listed on the monument, will be awarded a medal. 3. Monument: 1. All individuals who donate more than 100 yuan will be listed on the monument. 2. All members who, in addition to joining the association themselves, introduce 50 relatives and friends to join the association will be listed on the monument. 4. Acknowledgement: Regardless of the amount of donation, all donations will be acknowledged in the newspaper to promote benevolence. 5. Commendation: Those who solicit and raise more than 20,000 yuan, and donate more than 10,000 yuan themselves, in addition to being handled in accordance with the above regulations, will be submitted to the central government for commendation.

From February 1st 129

Silk fabrics will be increased in price.

Because the price of silk has skyrocketed, the sales are not enough to cover the cost.

The price increase method will be determined by each gang.

The Shanghai Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silk Fabrics United Association, in view of the current economic depression, declining sales, and sharp drop in prices, coupled with the soaring price of silk, resulting in sales that are almost insufficient to cover the cost, has repeatedly received letters from various silk fabric guilds in the two provinces, requesting a public announcement of price increases. Therefore, a joint meeting was held on the 19th of this month and it was resolved that all silk fabrics would be increased in price uniformly from February 1st. The method of price increase will be determined by each gang. The price increase notices of each association are recorded separately as follows:

United Association Announcement 130

For the matter of announcement, I recently received reports from various silk fabrics guilds in the two provinces, saying that the current price of silk has skyrocketed (factory silk has increased by 40 cents, and local silk has increased by 20 cents). As a result, the cost of silk fabrics has increased, and the sales price is too disparate. It should be discussed publicly, etc. In view of this, the association convened representatives of silk industry guilds from Jiangsu and Zhejiang on the 19th of this month for a joint meeting. It was publicly decided to publish in the newspaper that all silk fabrics will be increased in price uniformly from February 1st of this year. However, the situation of each gang is different, and the announcement should be published by each gang's guild, etc., recorded on file. Corresponding to the discussion, publish the announcement as above, I hope you will see it.

Electrical Machinery Industry Price Increase 131

It is found that the decline of the silk weaving industry in this city is entirely due to the impact of the tragic drop in the price of goods. In recent years, especially the soaring price of silk has increased by more than 40 cents, resulting in excessively high costs of making goods and heavy losses in secret. Colleagues feel the pain, which is really unbearable to imagine. In order to rectify the market price of fabrics and maintain the survival of the industry, this association convened the ninth executive committee meeting on January 19 and resolved that the spring plate of each goods will be increased by 30 cents for pure silk fabrics and 15 cents for artificial silk interwoven fabrics in accordance with the original price, in order to maintain costs. In addition, at this time of economic depression and tight monetary supply, all customer transaction funds must be cleared completely at the end of the month, so as to circulate funds and avoid excessive secret losses. All our colleagues, whether members or non-members, should strictly abide by the record on file. In addition to the separate letter, a special record is announced. Please understand that the customers of each gang will be allocated goods afterwards, and I hope you will do so, Shanghai Electrical Machinery Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association.

Contemporary Art World Authority 132

Professor Siren arrives in Shanghai

Hoping to complete his early history of Chinese painting.

The Shanghai Times reported that Professor Siren, an employee of the National Museum of Stockholm, Sweden, has been studying Chinese art for many years and is known as an authority in the contemporary art world. He arrived in Shanghai last Friday. Mr. Siren has been away from China for more than five years, and this time he intends to continue his research on Chinese language, history, and civilization, in order to complete his great work "Early History of Chinese Painting." The two volumes he wrote about paintings from the early Han Dynasty to the late Yuan Dynasty have been published in London. Commentators say that his dedication to Chinese art and his profound attainments surpass those of ancient and modern times. Mr. Siren said that since he left China, his Chinese has become rusty, and he has come again to review his old lessons. However, when he was stationed in Stockholm, he spent almost all his time reading and translating famous works of art and painting from the Tang and Song dynasties. He also said that Chinese painting emphasizes spirituality and does not emphasize ornamentation, just like music to us. China only had art after it broke away from copying nature. Chinese art is actually painting to write thoughts and express feelings. According to Mr. Siren, he recently traveled from Vietnam. When he was in Vietnam, the French authorities guided him to visit the Hanoi Museum and the sites where ancient monuments were excavated in Tokyo. Tokyo used to be a Chinese vassal state, so there are many ancient works of art with Chinese style. Recently, exquisite Han tombs have been discovered, which archaeologists are paying close attention to.

Various Provinces Drought Relief Association 140

Actively planning agricultural relief.

Continuing to hire inspectors in six provinces.

Designing the distribution of spring planting seeds.

The Shanghai Drought Relief Association for various provinces has been increasingly busy with relief work recently due to the arrival of severe winter. Furthermore, at a recent standing committee meeting, it was decided to plan the distribution of spring planting seeds in disaster areas next spring, and appointed newly hired foreign consultant Baker to be responsible for the design, so that in addition to work relief and emergency relief, agricultural relief can be carried out. The details are recorded as follows:

Baker and Eight Others Design Agricultural Relief 141

The severity of the disaster situation in various provinces last year was rarely seen in the last sixty years. After the establishment of the Drought Relief Association, in addition to the work relief being handled by the local authorities in each province to issue bonds or raise funds, the emergency relief was the responsibility of the central government and the association to raise funds and handle it. Now it has been gradually implemented. The most important thing is agricultural relief. Now, after investigation by the association, the disaster areas in various provinces are vast, and there is no grass in the farmland. In a blink of an eye, the spring plowing season is approaching, and the need for seeds is very urgent. The distribution of seeds must not be delayed. Therefore, the newly hired consultant Baker, as well as Chu Huiseng, Quan Shaowu, Huang Hanzhi, Guan Jiongzhi, Huang Bodu, Li Dachao, and Huang Yinzhou were elected to be responsible for the design. According to Mr. Chu Huiseng yesterday, the previous report that a seed research committee was organized was not true. The purpose of the current work is to plan agricultural relief, and there is no need to delay the research. Baker is currently investigating whether there is a surplus from the previous customs surtax and the US wheat loan, in order to report to the association as a reference for designing agricultural relief.

Continuing to Hire Inspectors in Six Provinces 142

After the association successively assigned investigation and relief personnel to work in the disaster areas of various provinces, the directors of each investigation and relief successively reported the work situation to the association. In order to understand the relief work in various disaster areas and supervise and urge them, President Kong specially appointed inspectors to visit the provinces. In addition to Cheng Yiqing and Feng Yangshan, who have been appointed to inspect Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, Wan Shuxi was appointed as the inspector of Anhui, Ye Jingcong was appointed as the inspector of Jiangxi, Shen Zuoding was appointed as the inspector of Hunan, Liu Guidian was appointed as the inspector of Hubei, and Huang Zhenying was appointed as the inspector of Henan and Hebei provinces. At the same time, telegrams were sent to the directors of investigation and relief in various provinces, urging them to strictly follow the principles of investigation and relief, strictly eliminate and relax, and report the actual situation of each county as soon as possible, so that it can be announced and the society can know it.

Relief Association Reply Regarding Tax Exemption Matters 143

The Relief Committee, yesterday consulted with the Railway Ministry regarding tax exemption for advance shipment of relief supplies, replied to the association in a letter stating: (Official title omitted) With reference to your association's previous letter, regarding the purchase of rice, flour, and cotton clothing for distribution in disaster areas, requesting the Railway Ministry be petitioned to issue a general order to all railway bureaus, that relief goods transported by your association, whether relief grain or relief clothing, be uniformly exempted from taxes and shipped in advance, etc., the matter was forwarded to the Railway Ministry for consideration and reply. We have now received a letter from the Railway Ministry, Reference Character 業, No. 100, dated January 22 of this year, stating that the request for a general order for free shipment of relief clothing and relief grain is inconsistent with regulations and cannot be granted. Upon investigation, rice and flour are fine grains and not included in the relief goods listed in Article 2 of the Railway Transport Relief Goods Regulations. However, the shipment of relief clothing or coarse grains can be handled in accordance with Article 3 of the said regulations, charged at 50% of the ordinary freight rate in cash. However, the type, quantity, and starting and ending stations, etc., should be listed in detail and forwarded in advance for verification and preparation for transport. Please check and inform accordingly.

Director Liang Shanglian of the Ministry of Industry's Commerce Department Speaks On 144

Commercial Policies for Relief

Implementing Control and Promoting with the Entire Political Power

Passively Promoting Domestic Goods, Actively Utilizing Customs Policies

In recent years, due to the economic downturn, the nation's commerce is on the verge of bankruptcy. A reporter from the Daily News recently (the 25th) specially interviewed Liang Shanglian, Director of the Commerce Department of the Ministry of Industry, to inquire about the content of the Ministry's relief plan. Mr. Liang then gave the following statement:

Causes of Bankruptcy 145

The causes of China's commercial downturn are extremely complex. To list the main ones, there are approximately several points: ㈠ The rural economy is bankrupt, and society has lost its purchasing power. ㈡ Domestic production is lagging behind, and there is an annual trade deficit, with much of society's circulating money being absorbed by foreigners and taken away. ㈢ International trade is underdeveloped, and the domestic market is mostly seized by foreign goods. ㈣ All products have lost their ability to be regulated. ㈤ In the past, foreign capital could not penetrate the interior due to underdeveloped transportation, but now they are using their superior transportation power to gradually expand and reach the countryside. ㈥ The customs has no power to manipulate and utilize [policies]. The above six points involve a very wide scope, so it is not a simple problem, and simple relief measures alone cannot be effective.

Relief Methods 146

Minister Chen (Gongbo) is very concerned about providing relief to national commerce. I myself am also very interested in research and have had lengthy and thorough discussions. I feel that the fundamental solution must start with control and must gather the entire power of the government to make overall plans, taking everything into consideration. Superficially observing relief methods, they only belong to the Ministry of Industry, and at most are related to the Ministry of Finance, but in reality, many areas are involved, such as railways, transportation, foreign affairs, and even military agencies, which are all closely related to this issue. In my personal opinion, this overall relief plan must be decided upon in principle by the Central Political Council, and then distributed to the relevant agencies for joint handling, so that it can be implemented with the highest political power in order to seek a complete solution. Localized action may not be of much benefit.

Commerce in Various Places 147

This year, commerce in various parts of the country has been shrouded in the shadow of the economic downturn. Places such as Tianjin, Beiping, Kaifeng, Zhengzhou, Taiyuan, Hankou, etc., are generally in the same situation. Rui Zengxiang, a store in Beiping that has been open for more than 200 years, has had its foundations shaken and is now being maintained by the Chamber of Commerce. In other places, many stores have also closed down and have been given relief by local political or commercial groups. Although this is not a fundamental solution, there seems to be no other perfect plan besides using this method. Last year, the overall business situation for stores in Shanghai was also mostly a case of losses exceeding profits. The declarations of liquidation or temporary closure of various companies are clear evidence of this. Others, such as flour mills and yarn factories, although occasionally there are profits, in essence, they are not true profits from the commercial enterprises themselves, but profits from commercial policies. The blow they have received is partly due to the economic downturn, but also partly due to the import and dumping of foreign goods. For example, the year before last, the national cotton harvest was abundant, but prices rose sharply. Last year, cotton production decreased, but prices fell instead. This is clear evidence of this. According to Gu Xinyi, manager of the Shanghai Grain Exchange, last year Shanghai ordered and imported a total of six million bags of foreign rice, worth seventy or eighty million yuan, which were all sold in the interior. With such a huge amount of money flowing out, society suddenly lost its ability to utilize it, and commerce naturally suffered a major impact. Shanghai's commerce is on the verge of bankruptcy, which is not due to this one reason alone, but it is also an important cause.

Promoting Domestic Goods 148

Promoting domestic goods is originally one of the methods for revitalizing commerce, but the word "promoting" is actually passive, not active. Passive methods have very little effect. Foreign goods can use dumping policies as a tool to break through. Active methods must rely on the use of customs policies, which is not permissible in the current situation. Therefore, although passive methods have little effect, they seem to be slightly better than no method at all.

Shanxi Example 149

Finally, when the reporter asked about Shanxi's economic control policies, Mr. Liang said that Shanxi's economic control had achieved considerable results, the most notable of which was the cigarette industry. Self-sufficiency was achieved, and the entry of foreign cigarettes was prohibited. Later, after protests from British and American companies, a compromise was reached, allowing the import of several hundred boxes per year, but the quantity was quite small.

Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs Plans to Formulate 155

Rural Cooperation Experiment Zone Plan

To Save the Rural Economy from Recession

Designating Yinhang District for Pilot Implementation

Central News Agency reports: The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, in order to save the rural economy from recession, and following the precedents of Denmark and other countries, has formulated a rural cooperation experiment zone plan and submitted it to the municipal government for approval. Once approved by the municipal government, it will be implemented according to the plan. The original text of the plan is excerpted below:

Location 156

The selection of a location is extremely important, and the following points should be noted: ㈠ The local farmers must have a higher level of knowledge and education must be more common (the vicinity of a location with a rural school is most suitable). ㈡ The location must be a central location, with convenient transportation, and easy to connect with other villages and towns. ㈢ The scope of the area should be within three to five li, and should not be too broad. ㈣ Based on the above reasons, it is proposed to designate Yinhang District for pilot implementation.

Organization 157

The experiment zone will be directly under the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, with cooperative instructors from the bureau rotating to work in the district. A Cooperative Experiment Zone Promotion Committee will also be organized, composed of local elementary school principals, municipal committee members, representatives of farmers' associations, and impartial people who are enthusiastic about the peasant movement, to handle various cooperative undertakings in the district and be responsible for promotion and organization (the charter will be formulated separately).

Survey 158

㈠ The survey methods will be divided into individual surveys and overall surveys. Individual surveys will cover matters such as the personal, family, living, and economic conditions of individuals. Overall surveys will cover matters such as the organization, production, and education of a village or township. The most important thing to note during the survey is the attitude of the surveyors, which should be amiable and approachable, and the language should be simple and easy to understand. ㈡ The survey materials will list the various materials needed in the form of tables and fill them out separately. The most important ones are divided into eleven categories: 1. Table of Economic Income and Expenditure of Farmers' Families for One Year; 2. Table of Production Conditions of Farmers' Families; 3. Table of Education Level of Farmers' Families; 4. Table of General Conditions of Farmland and Agricultural Production of Farmers' Families; 5. Table of Sideline Business Operations of Farmers' Families; 6. Table of Social Organization Conditions in Rural Areas; 7. Table of Educational Undertakings in Rural Areas; 8. Table of Production Conditions in Rural Areas; 9. Table of Economic Organization Conditions in Rural Areas; 10. Table of Sales and Purchase Conditions in Rural Areas; 11. Table of Customs and Habits in Rural Areas.

Propaganda 159

After the survey, propaganda work must be carried out. The organization of this propaganda must go through a long period of cultivation and influence, and cannot be effective with just a few words. It is planned to implement two aspects of propaganda: language and written. ㈠ Written Propaganda: Print the essence, benefits, and organizational methods of cooperative undertakings into booklets, slogans, and short articles, or pictures, etc., and distribute them to each household or post them in various places, so that farmers can have a deep understanding and knowledge. ㈡ Language Propaganda: Open-air speeches, roving propaganda, convening representatives of farmers from the entire district for talks.

Guidance 160

After the propaganda, guide their organization. Regarding guidance matters, the important ones are described below: 1. Guide them in preparing to establish a cooperative society. 2. Guide them in drafting the charter. 3. Guide them in the procedures for establishing a cooperative society. 4. Guide the society's business plan. 5. Guide the society's business direction. 6. Other guidance matters.

Organization 161

The rural situation in this city is slightly different from the interior, so the undertakings of its organization should be determined with reference to the actual situation. It is planned to first carry out those that are practical and suitable for the rural environment of this district. Regarding the organizational methods, it is planned to adopt a multi-business approach, operating the following undertakings so that they can develop mutually: ㈠ Rural Credit Cooperation: Rural areas in our country have always lacked sound economic organizations. Urban banks are mostly too busy to care about them, and pawnshops and pawnshops often engage in exploitation and usury. Other institutions such as money clubs also inevitably have certain shortcomings and abuses. Credit cooperatives are the most complete rural economic organization, and they have two advantages: 1. They can provide small loans in installments; 1. They can absorb small deposits in installments, thereby connecting the activities of the rural economy, cultivating the virtues of diligence and thrift, and eliminating the exploitation of high-interest loans. ㈡ Rural Sales and Purchase Cooperation: Farmers' various supplies are mostly purchased indirectly from intermediaries, and the prices and quality of goods are often deceived. As for the sale of agricultural products, because the quantity is small, they cannot directly trade with factories, and trading and transportation are inconvenient. Every time they are monopolized by unscrupulous merchants and peddlers, the losses of farmers are even greater. Now, if we want to obtain low-priced and high-quality goods and eliminate the monopoly of intermediaries, organizing purchasing and sales cooperatives can obtain various benefits. ㈢ Rural Grain Storage Cooperation: The theory of storing grain for disaster prevention has recently become widespread, but the fundamental method is to organize a grain storage cooperative. It benefits oneself and others, uses each other, and there is no fear of disaster. It can also regulate the quantity and price of the market so that it will not be manipulated by unscrupulous merchants. ㈣ Rural Side Occupations: Natural disasters and man-made disasters are difficult to predict. Preventing them before they happen requires proactive measures. Otherwise, once a disaster strikes, they will become starving corpses. Therefore, farmers should also engage in other side occupations in addition to agricultural work, such as weaving, raising fish, pigs, chickens, ducks, knitting handicrafts, etc., to make up for the inadequacy of the income from their main occupation, and sometimes it is greater than the main income from agriculture, which should be promoted and organized as soon as possible. Regarding agricultural production cooperatives, the use of cooperatives is planned to be promoted in the second step.

Training 162

All good systems, without suitable talents, cannot have excellent performances. The people of our country lack sufficient understanding of the cooperative system. Once they are rashly asked to handle it, it will naturally be difficult to achieve results. Therefore, the cultivation of talents cannot be delayed. Therefore, a cooperative business lecture hall or training class is attached to this district to train cooperative talents and increase the development of cooperative businesses.

Supervision 163

Looking at the cooperative societies in various places recently, many abuses have occurred. Their organization is not sound, and a lack of supervision is also one of the important reasons. Therefore, after the establishment of a cooperative society, the supervision method should be strict. The cooperative society should report the various conditions in the society once a month. The competent authority will send personnel to supervise the business situation and accounting books at any time.

Jiang Jiangshi Requests 166

Qiu Changsheng to Return to the Clan

Filing a Lawsuit to Confirm Parentage

Qiu Weiqing, who started his business by operating pigments, left a substantial inheritance after his death, all of which is controlled by his son, Qiu Changsheng. Two years ago, Qiu's family members, due to disputes over property division, sued Changsheng in the First Special District Local Court, stating that Changsheng was not Weiqing's biological son, but a foster child since childhood. The lawsuit lasted for a long time and was eventually settled through mediation. Now, Jiang Jiangshi, a 65-year-old woman from Jiangdu, has come forward to admit that Changsheng was born to her and asked Changsheng to recognize his ancestors, thus confirming the question of whether Changsheng is Weiqing's biological son. However, Changsheng is now enjoying a life of affluence and will not abandon his wealthy status to follow a poor woman back to her hometown. He absolutely denies that Jiang Jiangshi is his biological mother. The woman presented a petition to the First Special Court, claiming that a son should not be ungrateful and could not forget his parents' boundless kindness. She stated that her late husband, Xianxiang, due to the decline of the family and the difficulty of raising children, entrusted his biological son Changsheng to Qiu Weiqing in the same village with the introduction of Mr. Xu Zhen, a director of the village, in the 31st year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty. Later, the Qiu family took their family and Changsheng to Shanghai for business, and her late husband died soon after. The second son also died. At that time, she knew that the Qiu family already had children, so she came to Shanghai in August of the 21st year to have Changsheng return to the clan. At that time, the Qiu family was experiencing domestic disputes, and it was difficult for Changsheng to move elsewhere. She was persuaded by mediators to postpone it for one or two years, which she thought was reasonable, so she let it be delayed until today. Unexpectedly, Changsheng has recently turned against her and acted as if they were strangers. Considering her age and her eagerness to see her son, she petitioned the court to summon Changsheng for mediation and persuade him to return to the clan in order to preserve the bloodline of the Jiang family. The court has already held a hearing for mediation, but because it was ineffective, Jiang Jiangshi hired attorney Chen Daxun to file a lawsuit to confirm parentage. The day before yesterday afternoon, Judge Peng Shi summoned the defendant for trial, but he failed to appear. Jiang Jiangshi stated the circumstances of the Qiu family's adoption and the circumstances of being persuaded to postpone the order to return to the clan in Shanghai the year before last. Bu Shaoru and lawyer Wang Siji, gentry and merchants from Jiangdu who were traveling in Shanghai, both participated in the mediation and asked to summon the two men to the case, which would be able to prove [the truth]. Judge Peng then ordered a change of date to summon the witnesses for further questioning.

Robbery at the Huadong Manufacturing Factory 167

Thieves Opened Fire and Resisted Arrest

Vigilant Members of the Defense Corps Surrounded and Arrested

Seven Thieves Escaped, Factory Did Not Suffer Any Losses

At about 4 a.m. yesterday morning, seven armed thieves at the Huadong Manufacturing Factory at the intersection of the Lincolns Branch Road in Xinjing, Northwest Shanghai, pulled open the bamboo fence gate and sneaked in, then broke the glass window and climbed into the factory, going straight to the bedrooms of the factory manager Huang Xishan and others. All the employees were awakened. Just as the thieves were about to commit robbery, they were spotted by a passerby outside the factory, who reported the thieves' actions to Gong Yifei, a member of the First Defense Team of the Puzong District Gongjiazhai Defense Corps. After receiving the report, Gong immediately led eight armed corps members to the Huadong Manufacturing Factory to surround and arrest the thieves. Knowing that things were not going well, the thieves turned around and rushed to escape, taking the initiative to fire a pistol to resist arrest and demonstrate. Corps member Gong and others followed them in the dark, chasing and arresting them all the way, and also fired three shots in retaliation, but fortunately no one was injured. As a result, the thieves took the opportunity to flee east along the Lincoln Road without a trace. Afterwards, the factory reported the incident to Wang Dasui, Director of the Caojiadu Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who sent personnel to investigate. After receiving the report, Director Wang sent Inspector Long to investigate. The factory did not suffer any losses and reported the incident to the headquarters for record.

Murder of Indian Constable Case 168

Witnesses Summoned to Court

Two Indian Constables and a Teahouse Worker Testified in Court

Luo Xinfa Stated Insistently That It Was Someone Named Bao

At 10:45 p.m. on the ninth day of the tenth month of last year, Indian Constable No. 258 of the Public Concession Police was patrolling the Hejian Road when he was shot and killed in a vital area. Afterwards, Chinese Detectives Liu Wenzao and Su Yinggen arrested two suspects, Zhou Hongtian and Wang Jinsheng, both from Taizhou. Wang confessed that the pistol used to shoot the Indian constable belonged to Wang Jinfa (i.e., Luo Xinfa), a thief arrested by the French Concession. The pistol was then brought in and verified to be genuine. The two criminals, Zhou and Wang, were escorted to the First Special District Court and interrogated several times. Initially, they pushed the blame on each other, but then they jointly retracted their confessions, claiming that the real murderer was someone named Bao who was on the run. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. The day before yesterday, Judge Wu Zehan visited the Criminal Third Court for investigation. Lawyer Li Zhishan of the Public Works Department stated that today there are two Indian constables and a teahouse worker from Room 20 of the Huidong Hotel on Route Doumer, where the defendant stayed before the incident, to testify. Luo Xinfa also made a proposal. According to Luo, the pistol from the White Russia Road robbery case in the French Concession was handed over to him near the Great World by someone named Bao, who was on the run, on the evening of December 16 of last year, and he went to rob with Wang Jinsheng. He did not know about the shooting of the Indian constable. The court read out the words from his confession in the Second Special Court that the pistol was given to Wang Jinsheng and handed over at the corner of White Russia Road, and Zhou went to rob. Luo replied that he was being falsely accused. According to Indian Constable Dai Jiaxing, who was a horse patrolman, he was patrolling the area when he saw Indian Constable No. 258 lying on the ground after being shot. He was still able to speak and said that he was shot in the back by a robber. According to Da Jiaxing, who worked as a supervisor at a factory at No. 55 Huaji Road, he rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm and Indian Constable No. 256 was already sleeping on the ground. He said that he was robbed and injured by a Chinese person who fled, and did not say how many people there were. According to Yin Ziwen, a teahouse worker at the Huidong Hotel, the two defendants came with a man and a woman on the 3rd of this month and stayed in Room 20. They left early and returned late. They went out on the evening of the 9th and did not know when they returned to the hotel. When questioned, the two defendants insisted that the one who shot the Indian constable that night was Bao, and the rest of their confessions were vague. Judge Wu ordered them to be taken back into custody and set a date for sentencing.

The Zhabei Water and Electricity Company of this city, due to the development of business and the increasing load in recent years, the power plant equipment urgently needs to be expanded. Xihu Road Engineering Office 171

Constructing the Xicheng Road Project

The Xicheng Highway is the only transportation route between Wuxi and Jiangyin. It has been contracted by the Xicheng Long-Distance Bus Company, which specializes in operating long-distance buses. The business is relatively developed, but the roadbed construction is not solid, and maintenance is not good, resulting in the roadbed collapsing and being uneven. Whenever it rains, the wheels turn into muddy ditches. In addition, the company's vehicles are old and often have accidents such as overturning and injuring people. Transportation has not yet been perfected. Now, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction, seeing this, has specially allocated funds to build a macadam road surface. Now, the Xihu Road Engineering Office is handling it nearby. According to the person in charge of the Xihu Road Engineering Office, since the road started construction in early December of last year, the project has been progressing rapidly. The section from Wuxi to Yanqiao can be completely paved within the month. Travelers are all praising the change from rugged to smooth. However, due to poor maintenance, the original roads and ditches on both sides have been occupied by villagers, who are farming mulberry and wheat. As a result, when the road surface is being built, the villagers often misunderstand that the mulberry and wheat are being damaged, causing disputes. In fact, the land on both sides of the roadbed was originally the roads and ditches for the earth base, which have been measured and priced by the Wuxi County Government and belong to the roadbed area.

Joint Transportation Handled by Two Railways and Two Companies 172

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, along with the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department's Highway Administration's Beijing-Wuhu Line, the Anhui Province Beijing-Wuhu sections of long-distance bus companies, and the commercially operated Jiangnan Railway Company, etc., have jointly implemented passenger intermodal transportation. Yesterday, a notice was issued stating that for the convenience of passengers, this railway and the aforementioned companies will handle passenger and baggage intermodal transportation, issuing first, second, and third class single and round-trip intermodal tickets. "Intermodal station routes" include the Shanghai North Station, Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, and Zhenjiang on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, the Wuhu Dongmen Bay location of the Jiangnan Railway Company, Yicheng Sunjiabu, from various intermodal stations along the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway to Nanjing Station, transferring to the bus route, passing through Wuhu Jiangbian Station, and arriving at various intermodal stations of the Jiangnan Railway Company.

Court Issues Warrant for Arrest 177

Flower Association Offender Xu Changrong

Cash Guarantee of Four Thousand Yuan Confiscated

Xu Changrong, a local resident nicknamed "Xu Xiaokai," was the accountant for a large flower association. In the autumn of the 22nd year [of the Republic], he was arrested by the French police and transferred to the Special No. 2 Court for prosecution. After investigation, he was sentenced to one year and six months in prison, with a fine of two thousand yuan. Xu, dissatisfied, repeatedly appealed to the High Third Branch Court and the Supreme Court, hoping to reduce his sentence. The Supreme Court upheld the original judgment. During the appeal period, Xu was detained in the detention center. Due to illness, he applied for suspension of detention and was released on bail for medical treatment. After examination by a doctor appointed by the High Third Branch Court, Xu was allowed to provide a cash guarantee of four thousand yuan and a shop guarantee to ensure his availability for questioning. Xu's family then paid the deposit and found a shop guarantor to bail him out. Now Xu learned of the final judgment of the Supreme Court, still unconvinced. He submitted another petition to the High Third Branch Court, requesting a retrial. It is now learned that the High Third Branch Court received the judgment and case files from the Supreme Court. The execution division issued a warrant to Xu Changrong to appear in court for execution the day before yesterday. Xu still claimed to be ill and receiving treatment in the hospital, refusing to appear. The execution division ruled that Xu Changrong's cash guarantee of four thousand yuan be confiscated, and issued an arrest warrant, ordering Xu's guarantor to appear in court and bring Xu in for execution within a specified time.

Newly Invented Yu-Style Typewriter 179

Wax Paper Stencil Printing Successful

The Yu-style Chinese typewriter, which has been granted a patent certificate by the Ministry of Industry, has been repeatedly improved. It uses steel-cast characters, with a hardness approaching that of copper. The machine is sensitive, and with a little practice, one can type thirty characters per minute, making sixteen copies at once. Recent experiments have shown that typing on dual-purpose wax paper and printing with a mimeograph machine can produce tens of thousands of copies, and the text remains clear. It is extremely suitable for schools to mimeograph lecture notes and announcements, being the most economical and efficient method. It has been purchased by Central, China, Agricultural and Industrial, Continental, Dazhong, Xinhua, Zhejiang Industrial, and other banks, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Ministry of Finance, and various national agencies, law schools, and commercial firms, with over five hundred units adopted. Those who have purchased it have praised it unanimously. It is heard that the inventor, Mr. Yu Jun Binqi, in order to popularize this tool for improving culture, is offering a special discount of 15% off the list price of three hundred yuan to purchasers, including all shipping fees for distant locations, and a ten-year warranty. If the typewriter is returned after ten years, it is still worth one hundred yuan. The manufacturing plant is located at 622 Zhoujiazui Road, Shanghai. Those who wish to visit or request samples are most welcome.

Robbery Occurs on Caishi Street

Zhang Guangzhou's Tragic Death Case Scheduled for Sentencing 183

Debate Concluded, Defendant Remanded Pending Decision

Zhang Guanghua, a native of Henan, age 27, and his 18-year-old younger brother Zhang,

Lived in the attic room of the three-story building owned by Old Woman Dai Chen of Ningbo, at number 24. Guanghua worked at the Shanghai Navigation Bureau on the Sichuan Road Enterprise Bank building. On November 22nd of last year, he took a break from work. Zhang Guanghua returned home and told the sub-letter he was ending the lease. He was preparing to return to his hometown, unexpectedly that night Zhang Guangzhou was suddenly killed by having his neck severed. Zhang Guanghua also suffered knife wounds to his head and jumped out of the window, shouting for help. The sub-letter contacted police, who brought Guanghua to the police station and transferred him to the hospital for treatment. Meanwhile, the police sent Guangzhou's body to the coroner's office. After verification by the court, as there were no other relatives in Shanghai, the body was buried by the charity hall. After Guanghua's knife wounds healed, he was brought back to the police station for investigation. The results showed that the deceased Guangzhou tried to kill his elder brother with a knife, and Guanghua seized the knife and killed him in self-defense. Guanghua was transferred to the Special No. 2 Court, and the police department's lawyer filed a public prosecution for murder. Judge Xiong Huiping held repeated hearings. Zhang Guanghua vehemently denied killing his younger brother and hired a lawyer to defend him. For the sake of caution, the judge personally went to the scene of the incident to investigate and brought all the books and documents from Zhang's house to the court for strict review, rescheduling the hearing. The day before yesterday, Judge Xiong held another hearing. The defendant's testimony was the same as in previous hearings. At this point, the court considered the investigation of facts and evidence to be complete and ordered the start of the debate. The police lawyer Gu Shouxi and the defendant's defense lawyer debated with each other for an hour. The court announced the conclusion of the debate and scheduled the sentencing for the 30th. The defendant was still remanded pending the decision.

National Mining Association Seeks Members' Opinions 188

On Banning Unlicensed Small Mines

Ministry of Industry Agrees to Formulate Careful Banning Measures

Hoping Everyone Will Contribute as Much as Possible for Review

The Industrial Association says that the National Mining Association, according to proposals from its members, the United Office of China Fu companies, Zou Le, Jinbei, Baojin, and other coal mining companies, has submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry to rigorously formulate measures to ban unlicensed small mines, in order to maintain mining rights and ensure safety. However, the mining areas of each are different, and the situations also vary. To understand the crux of the matter, an on-the-ground investigation is necessary. The Ministry of Industry, in view of the deep and great future of the overall mining industry development, has instructed the association to ask its members for detailed opinions, collect them, and submit them to the ministry for reference and review. After receiving the Ministry of Industry Mining Character No. 10595 approval, the association immediately sought the opinions of its members. The Ministry of Industry's approval and the association's request for member opinions are recorded separately below.

Ministry of Industry Approval 189

All submitted items have been noted. Previously, the association submitted a request for strict banning of small mines. An order was issued to the responsible authorities in each province and city to handle applications for small mines carefully and not to issue licenses indiscriminately. The existing small mines that had obtained mining rights should also be supervised and guided at any time. Subsequently, the responsible authorities in each province and city submitted reports one after another, stating that they had earnestly followed the previous order. Even Shanxi, which has the most small mines, has established restrictions on small mines along railway lines and has obtained approval for implementation. It can be seen that the Ministry's banning of small mines has been actively carried out, and each province is gradually achieving visible results. The standard for the approval of small mining rights, according to Article 59 of the Mining Law, requires that the small mine be located in an area with inconvenient transportation, or with very small mineral resources, or in an undeveloped mining area, before mining rights can be established. Therefore, within the established mining areas of large coal mines in various provinces, such as near Zhongxing, Liuhegou, Cixian, Lincheng, Jiawang, Zou Le, Zhongyuan, as well as Kailuan, Luda, and other mining areas, the Ministry has not approved the establishment of small mining rights by the people, always aiming to maintain the main purpose of large mines, in order to protect mining interests. Those who are mining small mines near large mines without submitting for approval should be regarded as private mining behavior, and most are inherited earth kilns. The large mine itself can report to the responsible authorities in each province according to law, and the Ministry has been very strict in handling cases of private mining recently, repeatedly ordering the responsible authorities in each province and city to investigate strictly, prohibit according to law, and take careful measures. It has now been reported that a request to strictly formulate measures to ban small mines has been received by the Ministry. The Ministry is now studying how to formulate these banning measures carefully. If each company of the association has detailed opinions, they should be immediately submitted to the Ministry for reference. This approval is hereby issued for compliance.

Request for Opinions 190

The association's letter to each member states, "Regarding the case of strictly banning small mines using indigenous methods, the China Po Le Coal Mining Company and the United Office of the China Fu Companies proposed one after another, and the association reported to the Ministry of Industry for approval, which has been separately ordered to the responsible authorities for supervision and guidance and notified to each. Subsequently, the Po Le Coal Mining Company sent a letter, requesting to submit to the Ministry again, to promptly and clearly define measures to prohibit small mines using indigenous methods. After reporting the circumstances earnestly again, we received the Ministry of Industry Mining Character No. 10595, briefly stating, 'The Ministry is currently studying how to formulate these banning measures carefully. Each company of the association should immediately submit to the Ministry for reference.' Therefore, in addition to sending a separate letter, the original submission and ministry approval are copied and sent together, hoping you will check and comply. If there are any opinions to be stated, please promptly prepare them in detail and send them to the association for collection and submission."

Municipal Party Headquarters Labor Movement Training Institute 191

Opening Ceremony Held Yesterday Morning

Chairman Wu Xingya Reports on the Significance of Opening

Wu Kaixian and Others Give Speeches Explaining the Labor Movement Guidelines

The Shanghai Municipal Labor Movement Personnel Training Institute, organized by the Municipal Party Headquarters, has been prepared and held its opening ceremony at Meijialong, Xiaonanmen at 10 AM yesterday morning, presided over by Institute Director Wu Xingya. The details are recorded as follows:

Participating Representatives 192

Present were Director Wu Xingya, Deputy Director Zhu Xuefan, Municipal Party Headquarters Supervisor Wu Kaixian, Executive Committee Members Tao Baichuan and Lu Jingshi, Standing Committee Members of the General Labor Union Zhou Xuexiang, Shao Xubai, Ye Xianggao, Long Peiyun, Meng Nan, Xiao Huqing of the Municipal Farmers Association, Hu Shouqi of the First District Party Headquarters, and representatives from various labor unions such as military uniforms, cotton spinning, water and electricity, soap and medicine, and medicine stores, including Lu Jiyun, Li Hua, Lu Yinchu, and over 300 students from the Municipal General Labor Union military training and labor movement training institute. Wu's Speech 193

Director Wu Xingya of the Seventh Labor Movement Training Institute reported, "Today is the opening ceremony of the Labor Movement Training Institute organized by the Municipal Party Headquarters. It is an honor to have representatives from various labor unions participating in the ceremony. Since the January 28th Incident, the labor movement has made considerable progress and foundation on the whole. In terms of passive work, the communists who used to parasitize on community groups and engage in destructive work have been completely purged, which should be attributed to the efforts of those who lead the labor movement. The labor movement policy is not limited to passive work, but should also engage in active work. First, train cadres and go deep into the ranks of workers, leading the workers with the spirit of hard work, sacrifice, and struggle to achieve labor-capital coordination, communicate the emotions of the workers, promote the workers' production technology, believe in our party, and obey the leader. Looking at the domestic rural industry and commerce, all are showing signs of depression. In the international capitalist arena, the emerging industries are fragile and cannot resist. If we do not seek relief immediately, and are instead anesthetized by reactionary emotional language, it will only hasten our demise. It is hoped that all students will serve in the ranks of workers after graduation and must be loyal to our party, loyal to the country, and loyal to the leader, to complete the work of the revolution. This is the purpose of the Municipal Party Headquarters in organizing this institute."

Representative Speeches 194

Wu Kaixian, Supervisor of the Municipal Party Headquarters, gave a speech saying, "The purpose of the Municipal Party Headquarters in preparing to establish a Labor Movement Training Institute is because it feels that there is a shortage of labor movement talents, not enough to allocate, so it hopes to create cadre talents to strengthen the force and to engage in the development of national capital in accordance with our party's labor policy." Subsequently, Tao Baichuan, Executive Committee Member of the Municipal Party Headquarters, spoke, saying, "The labor movement advocated by our party is to protect workers on the one hand and develop production on the other, standing on the position of developing production to protect the interests of workers, and standing on the position of protecting the interests of workers to develop production. Both are equally important. If we only focus on developing production and abandon the interests of workers, it is the proposition of international capitalism. If we only care about the interests of workers and do not strive to develop production, it is the proposition of the Communist Party. I hope that all students will do biological work entirely after graduation in the future, and at the same time, everyone should not forget the labor movement." Finally, Lu Jingshi gave a speech, and the music was played to complete the ceremony. Photos were taken, and the meeting was adjourned.

Training Courses 195

The institute's officials include Director Wu Xingya and Deputy Director Zhu Xuefan, faculty and staff Zhao Shusheng, Wen Zhuangyou, Zhou Yuwu, Liu Zhongyun, Wu Shuru, Xiao Qingshan, Dai Yongchan, Lou Lianze, Shui Xiangyun, Lu Yuanhu, Huang Xianggu, and Shan Pengfei. The training curriculum is divided into twelve areas: moral education, party ideology, politics, economics, history, geography, labor movement theory, labor movement practice, labor laws and regulations, investigation and statistics, legal procedures, official document formats, and military training. Classes are scheduled to begin formally today, with a graduation period of six months. Students with excellent grades in the future will be introduced by the Municipal Party Headquarters to serve in various labor unions.

Lawyers Should Use the Name on Their Certificate 196

To Avoid Misunderstandings

Lawyer Tang Deheng, with the courtesy name Gonglian, is a native of Yixing, Jiangsu. He joined the Shanghai Lawyers Association as a member in August of the 23rd year of the Republic and organized a law firm at Room 72, No. 416 Sichuan Road, practicing law in Shanghai. This time, while handling a case, he used the name Tang Gonglian, resulting in Lawyer Cao Lin finding no lawyer named Tang Gonglian and sending a letter to the Lawyers Association, accusing Tang of impersonating a lawyer and requesting a review. The association proposed a discussion at the 188th Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees, resolving to send a letter to the Shanghai First Special District Local Court Prosecutor's Office, requesting the Industry Bureau Police Department to investigate. Before this letter was sent, the matter had already been clarified: Tang Deheng is Tang Gonglian. The misunderstanding was due to the mistaken use of the courtesy name. The association now intends to notify all members that in the future, when handling cases or representing parties in newspapers, they must use their real name (i.e., the name on the lawyer's certificate from the Ministry of Justice) and never use their courtesy name again, to avoid similar incidents and misunderstandings.

Advancement of Business at Kailin Paint Factory 198

The Kailin Paint Company on Xitiyu Road was established in the fourth year of the Republic of China and has a history of nearly twenty years. The chairman is Li Runsheng, and the general manager and factory director is Zhou Yuantai. The factory site covers more than 30 mu, making it the leader among domestic paint manufacturers. Unfortunately, due to the January 28th Incident, the old factory at the intersection of Jiangwan Road and Tongji Road was destroyed by artillery fire, resulting in enormous losses. After vigorous reorganization, the current achievements were made. The factory's internal machine manufacturing departments are divided into ten departments, including: White Pigment Department, Colored Pigment Department, Red Lead Department, Kerosene Department, Varnish Department, Thick Paint Department, Improved Colored Enamel and Wood Paint Department, Colored Blending Paint Department, Drier Department, and Wall Paint Department, as well as various product departments related to paint. The pigment manufacturing department is the largest. The total power of the factory's electric motors is about 1,000 horsepower, with no fewer than 100 large and small machines. Due to the perfection of various equipment, business is progressing exceptionally.

Page 13

Zhabei Porridge Kitchen

Announced Closure Again Yesterday 199

Number of Refugees Increases to 25,000

Factory Unable to Accommodate, Gate Crushed

The Organization Has Decided to Resume on February 10th

Rice Tickets Will Be Issued Appropriately During the Closure

The Zhabei Charity Group started operating the second porridge kitchen on Liuying Road at 6:00 AM on January 1st. Subsequently, due to the sudden increase in the number of poor people drinking porridge, the kitchen was unable to accommodate them, and it was forced to announce a temporary closure starting on January 5th. Then, more than 20 reed sheds were added to the east of the factory, and stoves were added. On the morning of January 13th, it reopened. The situation was recorded in previous reports. Now, the porridge kitchen has only been reopened for two weeks. Unexpectedly, starting on the morning of the day before yesterday (26th), it suddenly announced another closure. The situation is described below:

Refugees Crush the Factory Gate 200

Since the porridge kitchen added reed sheds to the east end of the factory and added stoves, reopening on the 13th of this month, the number of poor people drinking porridge has continuously increased to 18,000 to 19,000. The group then increased the porridge to 40 shi, which was just enough to meet the demand. Unexpectedly, the number of refugees has increased more and more in recent days. As of the morning of the 25th, it has increased to more than 25,000. The factory is again unable to accommodate them, and the refugees, driven by hunger, still forced their way in. The factory gate was crushed. At that time, the situation was extremely chaotic.

Fortunately, No Food Scramble Occurred 201

Fortunately, the group had prepared in advance, increasing the rice for the porridge to 55 shi, and cooking 86 vats of porridge. Therefore, the porridge was distributed according to the list, which was enough to meet the demand, and a food scramble was avoided. After the refugees dispersed, the group felt deeply that the situation was dangerous, and the number of people was still likely to increase, which was worrying. Therefore, starting on the morning of the 26th, it re-announced the closure and posted a notice outside the factory. It was heard that many refugees still went to the porridge kitchen the previous morning hoping to get porridge.

Decision on Post-Closure Measures 202

A Datong News Agency reporter visited the person in charge of the group on Datong Road yesterday afternoon to inquire about the situation. It was learned that the group has decided to extend the period to February 10th (the seventh day of the first lunar month) to continue operations. During the closure, the situation of the refugees will be investigated, and rice tickets will be issued appropriately. It was also learned that when operations resume on February 10th, a restriction method will be set for the refugees drinking porridge to avoid incidents.
