A Review of the Gold Bar Market (Continued) 277

— He Boxiong

(2) Changes in Pricing Standards

Before the European War, London was the financial center of the world, and its economic power in the Far East was immense. Therefore, Shanghai's gold bar pricing was based on the British pound. After the outbreak of the European War, the finances of Europe were disrupted, and our country's gold bar pricing also abandoned the gold pound and switched to Japanese gold. By the end of 1931, after Japan abandoned the gold standard, the Japanese exchange rate fell sharply, and our country no longer opened Japanese exchanges. Shanghai gold bars then switched to the American exchange rate as the pricing standard. After the United States abandoned the gold standard in April 1933, until December of last year, the American exchange rate fluctuated unpredictably, and the future trend of Roosevelt's monetary policy was even more unfathomable. It was rumored at the time that the current currency would be devalued. Therefore, the Shanghai Gold Exchange, in order to prevent changes from occurring, passed a new regulation on February 2nd of last year, changing the basis to the British exchange rate to seek a new price for the American exchange rate. From the standpoint of stable value, the existing transactions would still be cleared according to the old method. Until March, that is, at the settlement of the March term, each gold bar was priced at US$240 as the standard. At the same time, a new method was created to change the calculation method for gold bar pricing. For each gold bar with a fineness of .978 and a weight of 8.525 Shanghai taels, starting from February 16th, the April term would be listed and held. At the time of settlement, each gold bar would be priced at US$346 as the standard. Therefore, the difference between the March term and the April term market prices reached more than one hundred yuan. According to the usual practice, gold bar pricing was based on the American exchange rate, with each gold bar valued at US$240. At the same time, the weighing of gold bars was based on Shanghai taels. At that time, the Executive Yuan issued an order to switch to market taels when new transactions began to be traded in the April term. The conversion rate of market taels to Shanghai taels was 85.25. On March 1st of last year, the United States officially announced the legal gold price, with each ounce at $35 and each US dollar devalued to 59.06 cents. Therefore, the new fineness set by the US dollar and the new weight set by Shanghai gold bars were mutually converted, and the calculation formula is as follows:

(240 + .5906) x .8525 = 346.427. Therefore, after the gold bar was re-weighed and the US dollar revalued, the new converted gold bar value was US$346.427 per gold bar. Because of this change, the method of calculating the gold bar pricing is as follows:

$346.427 ÷ (the market price of the US exchange rate on that day) = 1018.8 yuan (gold bar pricing)

On October 15th of last year, the Ministry of Finance, in order to prevent gold bar speculation, managed the buying and selling of gold bars and ordered that the pricing of gold bars must be based on the customs gold unit listed by the Central Bank. Each gold bar is equal to ten market taels, with a fineness of .978. Each market tael is equal to 482.2611 grains of pure gold, and each grain is actually equal to .064798918 grams of pure gold. Therefore, each gold bar is actually equal to 305.62 grams.

10 x .978 x 482.2611 x .06479818 = 305.62 grams

Now, one customs gold unit is equivalent to .601866 grams, so the number of customs gold units obtained for one gold bar should be 507.79.

305.62 / .601866 = 507.79 customs gold units (fixed number)

Suppose the market price of customs gold on this day is 1.949 yuan. Then the market price of the gold bar should be 989.68 national currency.

507.79 x 1.949 = 989.68 yuan

(3) Suppression of Foreign Exchange Gold Bar Speculation

On September 9th of last year, the Ministry of Finance instructed Shanghai banks to restrict foreign exchange trading. The general meaning of the instruction was: foreign exchange transactions, except for (1) those necessary for legal and normal business operations, (2) private needs in the 1934. At the same time, the Gold Exchange was ordered to crack down on gold bar speculation. All new transactions should be conducted in cash, and the use of foreign exchange pricing was no longer allowed. Therefore, economists convened a meeting and decided that the October futures trading should be extended to the end of October due to time constraints. Starting from October 15th, a new standard would be implemented, and the customs gold converted from world gold bullion would be used as the standard for pricing in accordance with the order of the Ministry of Finance. Unexpectedly, the Ministry of Finance then instructed that the old October transactions should be allowed to be extended for one month, and no new transactions should be made. Starting from that day, a new standard would be implemented, and the customs gold price listed by the Central Bank, calculated according to the London gold bullion, would be used as the pricing standard. After a resolution by the board of directors of the Gold Exchange, the November term would be extended for settlement from October 17th, and the December futures would be opened at the same time.

The reason why the Ministry of Finance cracked down on gold bar speculation was that in recent years, the trend of gold bar speculation on the exchange has been very rampant. The buying and selling of gold bars is actually unnecessary, relying on the whims of foreign exchange as a speculative trend. When the US dollar is high, people rush to buy, and gold bars rise accordingly. Conversely, they are afraid of being left behind, and gold bars fall again. In fact, it is like gambling, which only disrupts the gold bar market. Moreover, the power of foreign exchange is controlled by foreigners, so that in the blink of an eye, countless people are ruined. Therefore, it is necessary to resolutely crack down on it, not only to protect the lives and property of the people, but also to stabilize social finance.

Furthermore, the reason for cracking down on the use of foreign exchange for gold bar pricing and replacing it with the Central Bank's customs gold listing as the standard is that the Central Bank's customs gold listing is based on the London bullion and the market price of gold bars. In other words, gold bar pricing is based on the customs gold unit, on the one hand, so that the price of gold is placed under the natural state of gold and silver supply and demand in London, and is not manipulated by human forces. (London is where gold and silver mine owners and merchants gather, so its bullion value usually represents the natural price of gold and silver supply and demand.) On the other hand, the focus of exchange is shifted from HSBC to the Central Bank, so that the Central Bank's function in exchange is expanded, and the possibility of gradually controlling the price of gold is enabled. Having considerable control over the price of gold can stabilize it, not following the fluctuating US dollar. This not only pleases businessmen, allowing them to have a definite calculation of the value of their goods, but also establishes a glorious authority in our country's exchange industry. However, its complete realization still requires considerable effort. — January 9, 1935. (The End)

Finance

Unfinished Procedures for the Closing of Silver Firms

This year's sluggish market is unprecedented since Shanghai was opened as a trading port. Therefore, the turnover ability of various industries is quite difficult. Generally, silver firms concentrate cash but have no way out, which makes it difficult to bridge the gaps. The continuous bankruptcies of stores have been endless, and the indirect and direct burdens are mostly unavoidable. Therefore, it is expected that this year's big closing will be more difficult than in previous years. The market atmosphere is outwardly relaxed but inwardly tight. The open market rate for foreign exchange is still 8%, the same price in the morning and afternoon. The dark market is actually only quoted, not traded. Most people are seeking prudence and are unwilling to release funds rashly, so the market atmosphere is rather calm. The trading volume of clearinghouse bills and bank collections, due to the weekly holiday, has no news to report. The trading volume of call loans was over 1.3 million in the morning session for transfers, over 200,000 for new transactions, over 400,000 in the afternoon session, and over 50,000 in the Small General Association. The trading volume of foreign exchange collateral loans was only over 400,000 for redemption by money shops and over 600,000 for new loans. The remittances from various places were over 300,000. The collection of foreign public single bills by money shops was over 29 million. The annual settlement of other silver firms was over 2 million. The inflow and outflow situation is not very smooth.

Securities 280

Bond Market Trended Downward Last Week

From January 21st to 26th of last week, the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange experienced the final week of January futures trading. The environment was turbulent and fraught with disturbances. Although the surface silver exchange rate retreated to 8 *fen*, this was not related to the actual tightness of the silver market. The collapse of Tongyi Bank further exposed the cracks in the sluggish business climate. Observing the changing situation, which tightened and loosened unexpectedly, especially as settlement approached, was enough to incite infighting. With the Lunar New Year approaching and a long holiday period imminent, most traders were unwilling to hold positions for too long, fearing the dangers of changes during the holiday. Therefore, the March futures, which would be listed simultaneously with the reopening on February 8th for the remaining two days, were not expected to experience much price fluctuation. Over the past week, on Monday, it appeared that the situation would not escalate. However, the sudden collapse of Tongyi Bank raised concerns about potential repercussions in the silver market. Confidence plummeted, and large holders rushed to sell. However, the "Northern Faction" and "No. 16" groups bought in at the lower prices. Market prices rose slightly across three sessions, recovering somewhat by closing, but still down two or three *jiao*, to seven or eight *jiao*. On Tuesday, there was great hope for a peaceful resolution of the situation. The "Northern Faction" actively covered their short positions. Although many large holders also sold, the market saw demand exceeding supply, creating a slight short squeeze. On Wednesday, the "Northern Faction" and "No. 16" continued to cover, and market prices continued to rise, with the short squeeze intensifying, pushing prices up another three to five *jiao*, to seven *jiao*. On Thursday, a sudden conflict arose, and the news differed greatly from before. The market, which had just experienced a short squeeze, abruptly shifted to a long squeeze, causing a severe drop. The "Northern Faction" also sold heavily, leading to a sharp fall of two yuan at the opening. Although there was some rebound, the result was still a drop of several *jiao*, to one yuan and two or three *jiao*. Friday was the final day of January futures trading, and there was a renewed short squeeze, with prices rising by two or three *jiao*, to about half a yuan. On Saturday, only February futures were traded, and with the situation remaining unresolved, confidence waned, and prices fell again by three to five *jiao*. Overall, during the week, January contracts mostly rose by one or two *jiao*, to one yuan and one or two *jiao*, while February contracts mostly fell by one or two *jiao*, to six or seven *jiao*. The total trading volume amounted to 13,115,100 yuan. The resulting price changes are compared and listed on the left. (Unit: Yuan, Trading Unit: 100 Yuan)

Cotton Yarn 281

Foreign Cotton Mostly Fell Slightly

Yesterday, American cotton opened weak due to unfavorable news from Liverpool and sluggish spot trading. Prices for all months fell by four to seven points. After the market price declined slightly, dealers engaged in buying, but the volume of transactions was not high, so the range of fluctuations was not large. At the close, there was some short covering, resulting in a slight firming. Spot prices were unchanged, while futures prices fell by two to four points. The British cotton market was quiet and dull. Spot prices fell by two points, while futures prices fell by one point. Indian cotton initially strengthened due to short covering, but weakened later due to selling by European exporters. Bengal fell by three rupees, while Omra and White Broach both fell by one and a half rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left. (Telegram of the 26th)

Grains 282

Rice Market Continues to Plunge

Thick *Geng* Rice Down 1.3 Jiao, Late Rice Down 3-4 Jiao

(Hu Nan) Yesterday, the supply from various sources was slightly scarcer than before, with only about a dozen or twenty firms arriving (totaling over 6,000 *shi*). However, due to the previous slow sales of *Puzhongzai* rice, vendors, facing the end of the year, and having sufficient remaining stock, were eager to sell quickly, and had no choice but to lower prices to seek sales. This led to a revitalized after-sales market, allowing existing stocks to be cleared. As for orders from customers, the Qingdao and Yantai gangs continued to handle over 2,000 bags. As a result, prices for thick *geng* rice and late rice, among others, continued to plummet by as much as three or four *jiao*. However, the future market situation seems to have stabilized. Various grades of "Yinbianyuan" rice also experienced declines of two or three *jiao*, up to four or five *jiao*. "Duyangjian" rice was out of stock and had no market.

January

Limited Delivery Volume of Flour

Most Receivers Are Local Merchants

Radio Broadcast of Market Conditions on the Day

Yesterday was the delivery day for January flour futures. The overall delivery volume for the day was not brisk, as the goods from various factories were gradually taken away by customers. A portion was also withdrawn in advance for hedging purposes. As a result, only 22,000 bags of "Green Cannon Platform" from Xin Da were delivered, half of which were returned goods, and the other half were new warehouse receipts for the "Foot Pedal" brand from Fufeng, totaling 2,000 bags. The majority of the receivers were local merchants, while customers only took 3,000 to 5,000 bags.

The Happy Broadcasting Station of the local Lao Ximen (Old West Gate) has specially contracted with Zhi Shi Yong, located at No. 11 Xingye Lane, Tianzhutang Street, to broadcast flour market conditions. At 11:00 AM, it will report the opening and closing prices of the pre-market session. At 4:00 PM, it will report the opening and closing prices of the afternoon session. Those in the local and external communities who wish to stay informed about flour market conditions should tune in at the specified times for more detailed information.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Discussions

Another January 28th Incident 283

— Meng Ruo

Another January 28th! This painful scar, although three years have passed since that day, has not only failed to heal but has even worsened! The deadly blow the enemy dealt us was so severe! The spirit of our people has not died, and we will certainly avenge this humiliation one day!

The January 28th Incident was a conspiracy launched by Japan following the September 18th Incident. This conspiracy had a far-reaching plan. Not only did it have a far-reaching plan, but the plan was also consistent. Look! After the loss of the three northeastern provinces, Japan's ambitions were not satisfied, and they further invaded Shanghai. When the Shanghai Battle failed, they turned to seize Rehe. Later, they repeatedly disturbed North China and plotted to invade South China. And recently, Eastern Chahar is also in a state of emergency. The Japanese are using every means to plot against us!

After enduring the pain, the people of the country should have an awareness when commemorating this January 28th. That is, although the day of January 28th has passed, the tragedy of January 28th is in danger of being re-enacted anytime, anywhere. Not long ago, the Japanese army and navy stationed in Shanghai again conducted a large-scale armed exercise in the North Sichuan Road and Nanjing Road areas. About two or three thousand soldiers were mobilized at that time. Machine guns, armored vehicles, and tanks were all available. For a time, it shocked the residents of Shanghai. What was this for? It was a demonstration to our Shanghai people! The evening newspapers and the next day's newspapers recorded the incident, all using large-character headlines. One newspaper's title was very startling, writing: "The Tragic Scene of That Day Reappears Today."

"The tragic scene of that day reappearing today" is not necessarily impossible! If the national morale continues to decline like this, without a sudden awakening and revitalization, the future is truly dangerous!

Stepping onto Singapore 284

— Overseas Student

"Singapore! Look there; on the coast are such tall houses, cars crawling like frogs, crowds of people like ants:..." Standing on the deck, my friend S shouted childishly, while I noticed the flag of the British Empire planted on a skyscraper, swaying in the sea-scented wind, appearing particularly proud in the sunset. Standing there blankly for a long time, the Taikoo Steam Navigation Company's XX ship had already stopped, dropped anchor, and the whistle cried loudly twice, suddenly waking me up, "Hey! Get ashore! Singapore has arrived!" S carried his simple luggage, and I carried mine, one in front and one behind, going ashore.

The brokers of the hotels crowded the shore, rushing toward us together, shouting their hotel names. Although we were not familiar with them, we had heard that "Nantian" was the biggest and best. So when we heard the shout "Nantian Hotel! Nantian!", we let the Chinese man with the Malay face check our luggage and took a car to the Nantian Hotel.

Soon, the night hung up like a piece of black cloth.

Like every big city, Singapore comes alive at night. Isn't it? Every room in the Nantian Hotel is active. Mahjong, women, wine, cigarettes: ... the soul of Nantian woven together. Next door is a stage performing a famous Beijing opera, and you can hear the noisy sounds of gongs and drums passing by. On the street; cars, trams, lorries, blew past like the wind, followed by rickshaws and bullock carts. Movie posters appeared on the streets in the most dazzling form, Caoutak showing a film of Shepley! Alhambra showing a film of Garbo! Women's idol Shepley and men's object Garbo, are mercilessly stealing their audience in Singapore. And I, "Let's go to the movies!" I said to S, and hailed a rickshaw to Capital.

The wide roads were filled with countless crowds. A broadcasting machine outside the department store transmitted the songs most adept at by black American. The night news recorded the turmoil of Europe and the coming of the Second World War. Now, Singapore's naval port has been completed under the British Empire's painstaking management; the day the great war arrives, what kind of fate will this only metropolis of the Malay Peninsula encounter!

At midnight, returning to the fifth floor of Nantian from Shepely's laughter, having been at rest for two hours, S was already asleep. I pushed open the window, took a breath, and looked up, the sky full of stars shining like countless eyeballs. Occasionally, looking down, I saw a few rickshaws lazily walking on the deserted streets. In the corner covered by the shadow of the skyscraper, there were women selling their bodies standing against the wall. Oh! The impression Singapore gave me was so terrible! There were also ferocious Indian police, patrolling the streets all night, monitoring the actions of every unemployed person:...

Stepping onto the shore of Singapore, I only felt the terror of the metropolis, an uncontrollable tremor made me lose sleep all night, until the next day when the sunlight shone on the bed, S woke up and asked me in surprise, "Didn't you sleep?" I could only sigh.

Anchored at Night 285

— San Lang

It was midnight, the black sky hiding such vast black clouds, the distant little stars flashing as if shedding desolate tears, the violent wind on the sea, deeply showing that the winter night in the South was a bit cold, as the steamer had just sailed into Guanghai Bay from the vast sea, the passengers on the whole ship moved and stood at the hatch, carefully watching the luggage, while facing the violent wind stirring the bottom of their hearts.

What a windy night! I sighed so much, at that time, several sampan women desperately resisted the huge waves, dropping the ferry in front of the hatch of the steamer. Everyone, withstanding the huge wind and flying rain, jumped onto the small ferry.

My seat was beside the boat, so the waves in the dark night flew out silver white, one by one, rustling - what beautiful waves!

When I was watching such a spectacle, I unconsciously had the waves wet my face and clothes, facing the sea breeze mixed with fluttering drizzle, I felt even colder, and my body gradually trembled.

After about half an hour, our ferry berthed on the stone wharf, I jumped on the pier, where high yellow electric lights were hung high, you could clearly see those porters soliciting business, those noisy voices, I felt the terrible strange local flavor deeply.

- Sir - Hey - To Guanghai Bay or Guanghai City?

Several porters endured the cold, stretching and shrinking, surrounding me. I had already planned to call a porter to lead the way in my heart. In this dark night, the strange road is always terrible. At the same time, I secretly feared the tricks of those hooligans, because Guanghai City had been a world of thieves for several years.

- Hey! Does Guang Yuanlong of Guanghai Bay know?

- I know, it is the newly completed shop of Mr. Chen. I'll take you there.

A man in his thirties picked up my things and asked me to follow him. After passing through a memorial arch, he folded into the small road on Gao Shanfeng. At that time, I couldn't see anything, only some hideous rocks were moving in my eyes. No one was walking, no sound, I was shocked - could it be that he was taking me to the thief's den?

So difficult, after several crooked roads, and arrived at the dilapidated street, a long stone street. Looking into the distance are some new houses, very beautiful urban architectural production, but also in the bustling night market sounds. So, I was relieved that I had not been kidnapped by thieves.

When I arrived at my friend's house, I felt the wonder of the front and back of Guanghai Bay Wharf.

- It is a beautiful seaside little city.

The Taste of a Wanderer 286

— Wanderer

I deeply savor the taste of a wanderer:

Riding a huge ocean liner, drifting on the sea that overseas Chinese call the Seven Seas, watching the moonlight rise and fall on the vast, turbulent waves; sailing in a small Malay boat among the creek harbors of Sumatra, watching the tropical forest cover both banks of the open jungle floor; riding a bicycle winding through the Malay plains, watching the red tropical earth stir up dust and smoke under the scorching sun...

In China, I climbed the peak of Hong Kong's Victoria Peak, gazing at the gray, dim homeland across the water; in the famous Suzhou and Hangzhou, where the ancient Chinese soul resides, I deeply tasted the feudal flavor of this ancient land; in the sinful city of Shanghai, I observed the souls of fallen people in the dark corners of the city; and in my hometown, I was suffocated under the dark, giant palm of the ancient nation...

Whenever it is a quiet night, when loneliness bites into the depths of my heart, I often recall the taste of my past wandering, and a wave of melancholy and joy surges through my heart. Thinking of ceaselessly rolling in the crowd in a chaotic era, ceaselessly wandering in a corner of the globe, is already the destiny that history has bestowed upon me. In the future, in order to struggle on the road of life, wandering and drifting seem to never abandon me, and a wave of gray sorrow covers my heart. However, when I think of seeing all kinds of human conditions in constant wandering, and gathering the wisdom of the earth from every corner of the world, if one day I see the bright side of humanity from the struggle of life, then isn't this painful wandering a treasure bestowed upon me by fate?

I remember once wading through puddles of accumulated rain on a long journey through the wild forest paths of Sumatra, stepping through mud and knee-deep water in the wild forest for four long hours. Nervously fearing that huge tropical beasts would come out and bite people, listening to wild birds screeching strangely in the black, thick trees; step by step, sinking my feet into the mud and then struggling to pull them out, pulling them out only to fall back in, watching the setting sun approaching dusk, yet the vast path still showed no sign of people (except for our own companions). How excruciating was the anxiety and hardship at that time! But how pleasant is the recollection now! I think, without this trek, not only would my livelihood at that time not have been resolved, but how could such a profound understanding and love for the equatorial land have left such a deep mark on my life?

I also remember once going with a young companion in a small Malay boat to catch a market fair, rushing along the rapids in a limited time. In a narrow section of the river, suddenly a large wild tree fell from the bank, collapsing across our small boat with a crash like a landslide. At that time, the small boat was being tossed by the tree's branches, and it was almost overturned into the river. Fortunately, the helmsman was skilled in boating, and used all his strength to hold the boat steady. After calming our frightened souls and using the saw we had brought with us to cut off a section of the thick trunk, we were drenched in sweat, and let the boat pass through the gap in the sawn tree. We finally escaped the danger. However, afterwards, when I think that if the small boat had moved forward a little further, wouldn't two young lives have been crushed under that tree trunk? This shocking story makes my heart race whenever I think of it, and the fact that friends had tried to stop me from making this trip makes me not regret it afterwards. Because without this trip, how could I have gone deep into the wilderness? Without this trip, how could I have seen the more primitive faces of the native people of Southeast Asia? Without this trip, how could I have felt so much joy for the knowledge I gained that time?

In China, the benefits given to me by wandering are not few. In the teahouses of Suzhou, I can see the ancient soul of the long-standing nation; on the waves of the Pearl River in southern China, I can see the heroic soul of a nation from its flourishing to its decline; from the capitalist city of Shanghai, I can see the dark face brought about by imperialism...

In the quiet night, I count the joys and pains that past wandering has given me, and a feeling of life's contradictions is intricately woven into my heart. I have quietly thought: if this society can make reasonable adjustments, then in the future, wandering and working in the world, that bright and happy vivid taste will immerse me in it forever. Erasing the dark side, and bringing upward mobility, wandering will become another kind of taste, and I will sing the praises of the wanderer's work anytime, anywhere!

Let the taste of the wanderer pass from the net woven with joy and pain to the only joy, from the two faces woven with darkness and light to the only bright direction! Abandon the suffering of life's wandering, and face the future!

Yuanchang Yongsheng Joint Broadcast Patriotic Drama 287

Today is the anniversary of the "January 28th" Incident in Shanghai. All Shanghai Chinese business radio stations will suspend entertainment programs for the day. The Yuanchang Advertising Company Broadcasting Station (frequency 1120) and the Yongsheng Radio Station (1080) have specially invited Mr. Li Changjian to broadcast patriotic dramas. The schedule is as follows: from 9:00 AM to 10:45 AM, "Blood of the Northeast"; from 1:00 PM to 3:15 PM, "Peanuts"; from 5:30 PM to 7:45 PM, "Soul of the Nation"; from 10:00 PM to 12:15 AM, "Blood of the Northeast"; from 1:00 AM to 2:00 AM, "Night of January 28th". Yongsheng Radio Station will broadcast "Night of January 28th" from 12:00 PM to 1:00 PM, "Blood of the Northeast" from 3:30 PM to 5:30 PM, and "Soul of the Nation" from 8:00 PM to 10:00 PM.

"Blood of the Northeast" Plot

The enemy invades our Northeast. A group of passionate young people have no way to join the army. They join the volunteer army one after another. Set off to the front line. Serve the country. Xiao Gou is a patriotic youth in his teens. Finally abandoned his old mother and weak sister at home. Joined the army. Rushed to the front to fight the enemy, wounded and fought hard. Before dying, he shouted loudly: I would rather be a heroic ghost of the Republic of China. I never want to be a slave to a fallen country!

(For details of this play, please read the "Blood of the Northeast" script published by Yuanchang Radio Station. Send a letter with a five-cent stamp to Yuanchang and it will be given as a gift)

"Peanuts" Plot

Everyone knows that the country is about the public. Don't look down on Lin Ren, who sells peanuts. But he also has a patriotic heart. This time, when the bandit army attacked our country's territory, he was willing to throw away his peanut basket and do something big for the country. How great is this spirit!

Lin Ren's younger sister, Ruhua, is born a beauty. Because her brother wanted to work hard for the country. Therefore. She did not hesitate to sacrifice herself to approach the bandits. So that her brother could sneak into the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. When the two sides signed the Twenty-One Demands. He desperately destroyed the treaty. As a result, he was cut off his nose by the bandits. Eyes gouged out. How terrible and pitiful. Later, his sister finally avenged her brother.

"Soul of the Nation" Plot

Seeing that the country was in trouble, Zhang Tianhua did not want to see the country perish. So he joined the army. He said goodbye to his lover to serve the country. This scene made people sad. But his lover. It's also bloody. Determined to join the army too. Secretly protect his lover. In the end, he sacrificed for the country. Only then did he find his lover.

"Night of January 28th" Plot

The "Night of January 28th" Incident broke out suddenly. I don’t know how many people were killed. Old Zhao Fengting and his daughter Mei Zhen fled to escape. On the way, they encountered the corpse of their son Xiao Mao. Hit the vital point in the gun. The old man was crying in pain. He was hit and killed by stray bullets again. (For details and dialogue, see the second issue of Mimi Collection published by Yuanchang Radio Station.)

Shanghai Shenbao Local Supplement Film Special Issue

George Raft's Tuxedo Worth $3,500 USD 291

— Xuemei

Do you believe it or not, George Raft once spent $3,500 USD to make a tuxedo? But that is the fact. Let me tell you about it.

That was an anecdote from when George Raft was still humble, in New York. Few people know about it. Only now an old friend has told it for him. He is rich now, dressed neatly, walking out of his dressing room. He was wearing a dinner suit, and he met the old friend, and pointed to his clothes, asking him: "Look, how is it? Not bad, eh?" The friend said slowly: "Well, not bad. But, do you remember that $3,500 one?" After George walked away, the friend told the story of the $3,500.

Many years ago, when George was dancing at the Texas Guinan nightclub in New York, he took two weeks off after a period of hard work to rest. On the first night of his rest, he ran to a Kirkleigh gambling den on 56th Street. The dice were his own choice. He wasn't rich at that time, so the bets he placed were naturally small and very careful. But that day was the day that the God of Gamblers was taking on a disciple. George Raft was lucky in gambling, and after an hour, he had already won three thousand five hundred dollars. That was the most money he had ever won in his life. He was so excited that he asked a friend next to him, who is now telling this story: "What time does the boat to London leave tonight?" He said: "Twelve o'clock." George asked again: "What time is it now?" He said: "Half past ten." George quickly stuffed a large roll of colorful paper into his pocket, grabbed his friend, and ran out. He said: "I'm going to London tonight, I have urgent business!"

Without further ado, George did indeed take that boat to London. The reason why he traveled across the ocean to London, England, was only told by George himself after returning to New York. He said:

"I have a quirk, which is that I like to dress well. Where did that quirk come from? Let me tell you. At that time, I was dancing in various nightclubs in New York. Texas Guinan gave me something to do. She told me to meet her. I had never been to any high-class nightclubs, so I didn't know what was inside. So I tried my best to dress myself up, wearing what I thought was the most beautiful outfit - a purple shirt, plus a fiery red tie.

"When I walked into the nightclub, I looked around, and everyone was wearing dinner suits, snow-white hard shirts. I suddenly felt my face flushing. That red bow tie almost burned a big hole in my purple shirt. I looked around, found the nearest exit, and without meeting Texas Guinan, I quickly slipped out. From then on, I knew what it meant to dress in a high-class way. From then on, I got this quirk of being particular about dressing.

"Later, I also developed the habit of wearing dinner suits. Every night, I wouldn't dare to meet people without wearing formal attire. At that time, my only ambition was to wear the most exquisite tuxedo that money could buy. That night, I won three thousand five hundred dollars out of nowhere in the gambling den. I thought I was probably happy for a moment, and went crazy. I immediately thought of London, England, which is famous for making tuxedos, so I thought of going to London and having them make me the most exquisite tuxedo.

"So I took that boat to London and ordered a tuxedo from the most famous H. Huntsman & Sons clothing store."

Of course, a tuxedo wouldn't cost that much money. But when I returned to New York, I was empty-handed and penniless.

"When I was on the boat back, I won some games of billiards on the boat. When the boat left Southampton, I counted my money, and it had decreased by a bit, but there was still a full two thousand dollars, and a brand new tuxedo. I thought to myself, since I'm so lucky, why not gamble big. So I joined a poker game. Unexpectedly, this time was bad, I met the old ghosts. They gave me a big lesson. By the time I arrived in New York and got ashore, I was already a pauper.

"But not entirely. I thought I was a pauper, but after a while, I found a small ten-dollar gold coin in the pocket of the tuxedo. That was also the first money I had ever won at the Kirkleigh gambling den."

Film Reviews

Review of "Are We Civilized?" 292

— Ling He

"Are We Civilized?" / Da Guangming

I almost cannot help but admit to the readers that I was deeply moved by "Are We Civilized?" Although it still contains some shortcomings. (As for why the original name was translated into "An Anthology of Ancient and Modern Wonders," that is incomprehensible.)

The cruelty of the First World War left a very painful memory for the people of European and American countries. The war destroyed their homes, the war turned the world into a cemetery, and the war destroyed human civilization. Therefore, from not long after the war until now, we have seen many films about the World War, and among them there are many famous films against imperialist wars. Obviously, progressive, humanitarian filmmakers abhor war, and they oppose war, all of which are expressed in their works.

Now, twenty years after the First World War, the Second World War is on the verge of breaking out again. The expansion of armaments by various imperialist countries shows that the contradictions between them cannot be resolved without war. These have been seen by American filmmakers with a sense of justice, and their concerns are expressed in their works. In this regard, we can cite "The World Moves On" as an example, although it is a shortcoming of the work that it equates strengthening the armed forces for the sake of improving human life with the imperialist expansion of armaments. Now we have also seen Edwin Carewe's film against the Second World War.

So, let's see how he understands the true meaning of war? What attitude does he take to oppose war? From this point of view, give the work a proper evaluation. Here, the author is a righteous and humanitarian advocate for peace. He explains that human progress is from barbarism to civilization. And it is because of this civilization that the First World War was brewed, but this war destroyed the world's civilization. Now this barbaric Second World War is about to come again, so the author disguises himself as a scholar and preaches to the warmongers, painstakingly and sparing no effort to sacrifice himself, and as a result, the scholar's childhood friend, the general who holds military and political power, is also moved by him. However, this is precisely the shortcoming of the work. The outbreak of the war is by no means something that a small number of warlike people can create. Therefore, preaching to the officers here cannot eliminate war. Furthermore, the so-called peace between imperialists is the preparation for war, and true peace can only be obtained by eliminating imperialist wars through new and old wars. Therefore, the World War is anti-progressive, it is a barbaric act of civilized people, and the war to eliminate the war that hinders progress is what we need.

The work does not have a clear indication of these, which shows that Edwin Carewe is still stuck in the old worldview. Therefore, this is a relatively realistic work, but it does not penetrate deeply into the essence of reality in a critical way.

As mentioned above, perhaps this is too demanding of the author. To take a step back, it is very gratifying to see such a righteous anti-war work appearing in the United States on the eve of the Second World War. At least the author's attitude is very serious. It is a very clear fact that the author has adopted a very simple approach to express his own ideas completely, so we can certainly point out many shortcomings in the technology, but this is by no means a fatal damage to the work. The main thing is that in addition to the insufficient expression of the form, there are still some errors in the content.

Review of "Down to Their Last Yacht" 293

— You Jing

"Down to Their Last Yacht" / Da Shanghai Theater

The socialite Nila buys the only old yacht of the bankrupt girl Lingdai, and invites many dignitaries, wealthy merchants and magnates to travel to the South China Sea.

In order to maintain her livelihood, Lingdai still serves as a servant on the ship. Her lover Forbes was rejected when he asked to go with her, so he and his personal servant Freddie found a way to hide on the ship and follow her.

The shipowner intends to plunder the wealth of all the passengers, deliberately runs the ship aground, and goes to a deserted island to plan a robbery with the queen. Who knows that the queen does not lack money and wealth, but lacks handsome men. So among all the sailors and passengers who came to seek refuge, she fell in love with Forbes, this pretty boy, and wanted him to be her husband and king. She does not care whether Forbes is engaged to anyone, and orders all the natives of the island to open a celebration banquet for the wedding and abdication. Suddenly, outside the band, a man blowing a bugle appears, saying that he looks like her husband, so she abandons Forbes and desperately loves him.

The ship was playfully destroyed by the queen, and all the people were left on the desert island to live their lives of singing, dancing, love, and unbridled indulgence.

For this kind of story propped up by jade-like thighs, creamy breasts, singing, dancing, passionate love, and crazy kisses, we cannot make any more meaningful demands on it. General fragile and disillusioned people, when they are so disappointed with their lives that they cannot even trust themselves, try their best to laugh before death. Fantasy and fantasy, what absurd, strange, and arrogant things can't they think of?

In order to escape reality, reality gives these pleasure-seekers a more positive display, but fantasy is always being shattered. No matter how hard "Down to Their Last Yacht" struggles, it cannot avoid being stained with the atmosphere of similar films in the previous period. Primitive sexual love, from the rapid, wild, fresh, and unrestrained pursuit, has declined into a fluctuating, weak, old, floating, and astringent yearning.

From the handling methods to the tone and atmosphere shown, they are as described above. Not only is the large segment of shipboard life lackluster, but even the various things after arriving on the desert island are not flavorful enough. For example, a group of noble and gorgeous people stand on the ship's railing watching a group of naked men singing under the trees on the shore. That scene was so dull until the lengthy singing was over before there was some change. The queen's sensual performance cannot be well unified with the action. The turmoil between the natives and the refugees, individually and piecemeal, lacks splashing, open scenes on the screen, and the melodies lack the grandeur of the atmosphere.

Because the performers focus their efforts on singing and dancing, the actors inevitably lack outstanding achievements.

Li Lili's Love and Marriage 294

Li Lili's love and marriage have truly become a problem. Initially, in "Little Toys," she and Luo Peng were in love. In "Autumn Fan and Bright Lamp," it was almost because of Luo Peng's personality that the two got married. Now, in the "National Customs" co-directed by Luo Mingyou and Zhu Shilin, the love and marriage issues surrounding Li Lili are even more complicated. Originally, Lili was fond of Zheng Junli and finally she won and married Zheng Junli. However, not long after marrying Zheng Junli, Lili changed due to changes in the environment. Although Zheng Junli later almost went bankrupt providing her with money for education, she didn't care about it at all. As a result, Zheng Junli was abandoned. Who did Lili fall in love with? In the end, she still had a fate with Luo Peng. Because since they cooperated in plays, they have always played loving roles, so people generally say: "Lili and Little Luo can be called a pair of screen lovers."

Wang Huchen and Tong Yuejuan Leap onto the Silver Screen 295

— (Man)

The sound film "The Red Sheep Heroic Legend," which promotes the national spirit, is Xinhua Film Company's maiden work. It was informally screened yesterday, and reporters got a sneak peek. The actors in this film, such as Xu Qinfang, Tian Fang, Yan Ying, and Wang Zhengqing, all have enthusiastic voices and sincere expressions. Wang Huchen and Tong Yuejuan have transitioned from the stage to the silver screen. Stage plays and film plays each have their own unique position and nature. Wang Huchen plays Wei Changhui in the Red Sheep sound film, and Tong Yuejuan plays a wandering singing girl. They have completely shed their habitual postures on stage, which is particularly commendable. The most magnificent scenes include Wei Changhui's late-night visit to Hong Xuanjiao in prison to learn swordsmanship, and the burning of villages during the Jintian Uprising. The blazing flames, the impassioned military songs, and the earth-shaking sounds are rarely seen in domestic films. It is said that it will be released on the first day of the Lunar New Year, and it will surely cause a sensation among the people of Shanghai at that time.

Film Novel

The Red Sheep Heroic Legend (7) 296

— Zhao Chu

Outside Jintian Village, white cloth banners were hung, with the words "Welcome Mr. Wei Changhui" written on them. Many small flags and lanterns hanging under the eaves also had the same words written on them. Wei Changhui sat on his horse, looking around. Shi Dakai followed behind, urging the horse forward and pointing ahead, saying, "Brother Wei! The ones standing at the entrance of the village are Hong Xiuquan and Yang Xiuqing." Wei then looked forward and said, "Such heavy etiquette is truly undeserved." Upon arriving at the village entrance, Wei and the others dismounted. Hong Xiuquan stepped forward to greet them with great respect. Three cannons were fired, and music was played loudly. Amidst the enthusiastic cheers, they were welcomed inside. A banquet was set up in the hall, with Wei Changhui sitting in the center, and Hong, Yang, Zeng, and Shi sitting beside him in order. Hong Xiuquan poured wine and, holding the cup in his hand, said to Wei, "Today, we are honored that Mr. Wei does not despise our humble selves and joins our society. This is truly the supreme honor and is enough to encourage our fighting spirit." Saying this, he raised the cup and said, "Let's all drink this cup of wine and wish Mr. Wei good health." Everyone stood up and drank it all. After drinking a cup, Wei replied with a smile, "I am truly undeserving of such generous treatment from everyone. I am an ordinary person who originally wanted to do something, but I had no opportunity. Now that I have joined your esteemed society, this is truly the time for me to strive and be promising. As long as the mission of you brothers is within my ability, I will do my best to do it." Everyone at the table listened attentively. Hearing the last words, they all applauded and raised their cups to drink. At this time, the courtyard was crowded with people, and various lantern dances and acrobatics were being performed in the courtyard. The Beijing opera was also being performed on the stage. Let's leave the excitement aside for now.

It is said that one day, everyone was sitting and chatting idly in Jintian Village when suddenly a horse galloped in and dismounted at the village entrance. It was Qin Rigang, looking flustered and panicked. He rushed inside. Everyone was shocked to see Qin rushing in. Qin Rigang was distraught and unable to speak clearly: "Something bad has happened! Brother Hong Xiuquan has been arrested by the Guiping County government!" Several people stood up in shock and asked, "What happened?" Wei and Zeng also stood up and asked, "How could this happen?" Qin Rigang panted and said, "I accompanied Brother Hong to the county to take care of something. There was a yamen runner in the county who came from Guangdong. When he saw Brother Hong, he reported to the official, saying that Brother Hong had committed a crime in Huaxian, propagating the teachings of Jesus and plotting against the court. The county then sent yamen runners to follow us halfway and arrest Brother Hong." Xiao Chaogui was furious when he heard this and said, "This plague official dares to oppose us! Let's quickly kill our way into the city and rescue Brother Hong!" Saying this, he was indignant. Hong Xuanjiao also shouted, "Let's kill our way into the city today!" Yang Xiuqing and Feng Yunshan were both concerned when they heard this. Yang shook his head slightly and said, "Now is not the time for us to start an uprising. We cannot easily reveal ourselves." Qin Rigang hurriedly shouted from the side, "We can't just let Brother Hong be trapped in prison without doing anything!" Wei Changhui then said to everyone, "I have a plan, I don't know if everyone will agree. I know that the magistrate of Guiping County is a corrupt official. If we use more bribes, I can guarantee that Brother Hong will return safely." Zeng Wangheng listened and then said, "This method is the most stable. If it really doesn't work, then we will do as Brother Xiao said." Wei Changhui then cupped his hands to everyone and said, "The matter should not be delayed, I will go to the city immediately to take care of this matter." Everyone saw Wei Changhui off. Wei said to everyone, "Everyone, sit and wait for good news!" Saying that, he mounted his horse and left. As expected, money can work miracles. Hong Xiuquan was released from Guiping County thanks to Wei Changhui's rescue. Hong Xiuquan said to the crowd, "This time, we were fortunate to have Mr. Wei's help, otherwise, we would have suffered their poisonous hands. However, I think the government will find us sooner or later. We must be determined to prepare." Xiao Chaogui stepped forward and said, "We should kill our way out and seize Guiping City. Who can stand to be stifled here?" Feng Yunshan and Yang Xiuqing said, "Of course, we can't delay matters any longer. Now that the grain and supplies have been settled, we just need to wait for the heroes from all sides to be contacted, and then we can rise up in one fell swoop." Hong Xiuquan and Zeng Yuheng nodded in agreement and then said, "Now we can only intensify the training of soldiers and assign Dakai, Rigang, and Chaogui to be responsible, and they must not be negligent." (To be continued)
